## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
     2→// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
     3→
     4→package format
     5→
     6→import (
     7→	"fmt"
     8→	"sort"
     9→	"strings"
    10→
    11→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    13→)
    14→
    15→// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed, summary-style diff
    16→// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.
    17→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    18→
    19→// Format produces a compact summary of the given plan, showing one line per
    20→// resource change grouped by action type, followed by a summary count.
    21→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    22→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    23→		return "No changes.\n"
    24→	}
    25→
    26→	changes := plan.Changes.Resources
    27→	if len(changes) == 0 {
    28→		return "No changes.\n"
    29→	}
    30→
    31→	// Group changes by action type
    32→	grouped := make(map[plans.Action][]string)
    33→	for _, rc := range changes {
    34→		if rc.Action == plans.NoOp {
    35→			continue
    36→		}
    37→		addr := rc.Addr.String()
    38→		grouped[rc.Action] = append(grouped[rc.Action], addr)
    39→	}
    40→
    41→	if len(grouped) == 0 {
    42→		return "No changes.\n"
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	// Define action display order
    46→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    47→		plans.Create,
    48→		plans.Update,
    49→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    50→		plans.CreateThenDelete,
    51→		plans.Delete,
    52→		plans.Forget,
    53→		plans.CreateThenForget,
    54→		plans.Read,
    55→	}

96-assistanttext-
Both files are created. Here's a summary of what was implemented:

## Implementation Summary

### `internal/command/format/compact.go`
- **`CompactDiffFormatter`** struct implementing a plan formatter
- **`Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string`** method that:
  - Returns `"No changes.\n"` for nil plans, empty changes, or all-NoOp changes
  - Iterates over `plan.Changes.Resources` (the `[]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc` slice)
  - Groups resources by `plans.Action` type, skipping `NoOp`
  - Outputs one line per resource: `[action] resource_type.name`
  - Sorts resources alphabetically within each action group
  - Shows action groups in a defined order: create → update → replace → delete → forget → read
  - Appends a `Plan: N to create, N to update, ...` summary line
- **`actionLabel()`** helper mapping `plans.Action` constants to human-readable labels

### `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`
- Tests for nil plan, empty changes, NoOp exclusion, and each action type (create/update/delete/replace)
- Tests for multiple actions grouped correctly with proper ordering
- Tests for summary counts (`"2 to create"` etc.)
- Uses `addrs.ParseAbsResourceInstanceStr` to build test resource addresses
- Constructs `plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc` with embedded `plans.ChangeSrc{Action: ...}`

Encode(schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) (*ChangesSrc, error) {\n43: \t// a plan is always built even when there are errors, so make sure to return\n44: \t// a valid changesSrc.\n45: \tchangesSrc := NewChangesSrc()\n46: \n47: \tfor _, rc := range c.Resources {\n48: \t\tp, ok := schemas.Providers[rc.ProviderAddr.Provider]\n49: \t\tif !ok {\n50: \t\t\treturn changesSrc, fmt.Errorf(\"Changes.Encode: ResourceInstanceChange describes a change to a particular resource instance\n213: // object.\n214: type ResourceInstanceChange struct {\n215: \t// Addr is the absolute address of the resource instance that the change\n216: \t// will apply to.\n217: \tAddr addrs.AbsResourceInstance\n218: \n219: \t// PrevRunAddr is the absolute address that this resource instance had at\n220: \t// the conclusion of a previous run.\n221: \t//\n222: \t// This will typically be the same as Addr, but can be different if the\n223: \t// previous resource instance was subject to a \"moved\" block that we\n224: \t// \tPrevRunAddr addrs.AbsResourceInstance\n231: \n232: \t// DeposedKey is the identifier for a deposed object associated with the\n233: \t// given instance, or states.NotDeposed if this change applies to the\n234: \t// current object.\n235: \t//\n236: \t// A Replace change for a resource with create_before_destroy set will\n237: \t// create a new DeposedKey temporarily during replacement. In that case,\n238: \t// DeposedKey in the plan is always states.NotDeposed, representing that\n239: \t// the current object is being replaced with the deposed.\n240: \tDeposedKey states.DeposedKey\n241: \n242: \t// Provider is the address of the provider configuration that was used\n243: \t// to plan this change, and thus the configuration that must also be\n244: \t// used to apply it.\n245: \tProviderAddr addrs.AbsProviderConfig\n246: \n247: \t// Change is an embedded description of the change.\n248: \tChange\n249: \n250: \t// ActionReason is an optional extra indication of why we chose the\n251: \t// action recorded in Change.Action for this particular resource instance.\n252: \t//\n253: \t// This is an approximate mechanism only for the purpose of explaining the\n254: \t// plan to end-users in the UI and is not to be used for any\n255: \t// decision-making during the apply step; if apply behavior needs to vary\n256: \t// depending on the \"action reason\" then the information for that decision\n257: \t// must be recorded more precisely elsewhere for that purpose.\n258: \t//\n259: \t// Sometimes there might be more than one reason for choosing a particular\n260: \t// action. In that case, it's up to the codepath making that decision to\n261: \t// decide which value would provide the most relevant explanation to the\n262: \t// end-user and return that. It's not a goal of this field to represent\n263: \t// fine details about the planning process.\n264: \tActionReason ResourceInstanceChangeActionReason\n265: \n266: \t// RequiredReplace is a set of paths that caused the change action to be\n267: \t// Replace rather than Update. New Action\n328: //\t--------+-------------+-----------\n329: //\tCreate    true          NoOp\n330: //\tDelete    false         NoOp\n331: //\tReplace   true          Delete\n332: //\tReplace   false rc\n405: }\n406: \n407: // ResourceInstanceChangeActionReason allows for some extra user-facing\n408: // reasoning for why a particular change action was chosen for a particular\n409: // resource instance.\n410: //\n411: // This only represents sufficient detail to give a suitable explanation to\n412: // an end-user, and mustn't be used for any real decision-making during the\n413: // apply (\n419: \t// In most cases there's no special reason for choosing a particular\n420: \t// action, which is represented by ResourceInstanceChangeNoReason.\n421: \tResourceInstanceChangeNoReason given action.\n566: type Change struct {\n567: \t// Action defines what kind of change is being made.\n568: \tAction Action\n569: \n570: \t// Interpretation of Before and After depend on Action:\n571: \t//\n572: \t//     NoOp     Before and After are the same, unchanged value\n573: \t//     Create   Before is nil, and After is the expected value after create.\n574: \t//     Read     Before is any prior value (nil if no prior), and After is the\n575: \t//              value that was or will be read.\n576: \t//     Update   Before is the value prior to update, and After is the expected\n577: \t//              value after update.\n578: \t//     Replace  As with Update.\n579: \t//     Delete   Before is the value prior to delete, and After is always nil.\n580: \t//     Forget   As with Delete.\n581: \t//\n582: \t// Unknown values may appear anywhere within the Before and After values,\n583: \t// either as the values themselves or as nested elements within known\n584: \t// collections/structures.\n585: \tBefore, After cty.Value\n586: \n587: \t// Importing is present if the resource is being imported as part of this\n588: \t// change.\n589: \t//\n590: \t// Use the simple presence of this field to detect if a ChangeSrc is to be\n591: \t// imported, the contents of this structure may be modified going forward.\n592: \tImporting *Importing\n593: \n594: \t// GeneratedConfig contains any HCL config generated for this resource\n595: \t// during planning, as a string. If GeneratedConfig is populated, Importing\n596: \t// should be true. Pass the type constraint\n603: // that the values are expected to conform to; to properly decode the values\n604: // later an identical type constraint must be provided at that time.\n605: //\n606: // Where a Change is embedded in some other struct, it's generally better\n607: // to call the corresponding Encode method of that struct rather than working\n608: // directly with its embedded Change.\n609: func (c *Change) Encode(ty cty.Type) (*ChangeSrc, error) {\n610: \t// We can't serialize value marks directly so we'll need to extract the\n611: \t// sensitive marks and store them in a separate field.\n612: \t//\n613: \t// We don't accept any other marks here. (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed, summary-style diff\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format produces a compact summary of the given plan, showing one line per\n// resource change grouped by action type, followed by a summary count.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\tchanges := plan.Changes.Resources\n\tif len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tgrouped := make(map[plans.Action][]string)\n\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\tif rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\taddr := rc.Addr.String()\n\t\tgrouped[rc.Action] = append(grouped[rc.Action], addr)\n\t}\n\n\tif len(grouped) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Define action display order\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf strings.Builder\n\tvar summaryParts []string\n\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\taddrs, ok := grouped[action]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Strings(addrs)\n\t\tlabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\tfor _, addr := range addrs {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"[%s] %s\\n\", label, addr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsummaryParts = append(summaryParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to %s\", len(addrs), label))\n\t}\n\n\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"Plan: %s.\\n\", strings.Join(summaryParts, \", \"))\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"update\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"delete\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"read\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"change\"\n\t}\n}\n",

plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"delete\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"read\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"change\"\n\t}\n}\n",

    "content": "// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed, summary-style diff\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format produces a compact summary of the given plan, showing one line per\n// resource change grouped by action type, followed by a summary count.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\tchanges := plan.Changes.Resources\n\tif len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tgrouped := make(map[plans.Action][]string)\n\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\tif rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\taddr := rc.Addr.String()\n\t\tgrouped[rc.Action] = append(grouped[rc.Action], addr)\n\t}\n\n\tif len(grouped) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Define action display order\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf strings.Builder\n\tvar summaryParts []string\n\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\taddrs, ok := grouped[action]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Strings(addrs)\n\t\tlabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\tfor _, addr := range addrs {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"[%s] %s\\n\", label, addr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsummaryParts = append(summaryParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to %s\", len(addrs), label))\n\t}\n\n\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"Plan: %s.\\n\", strings.Join(summaryParts, \", \"))\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"update\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"delete\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"read\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"change\"\n\t}\n}\n",

1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed, summary-style diff
// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format produces a compact summary of the given plan, showing one line per
// resource change grouped by action type, followed by a summary count.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return "No changes.\n"
	}

	changes := plan.Changes.Resources
	if len(changes) == 0 {
		return "No changes.\n"
	}

	// Group changes by action type
	grouped := make(map[plans.Action][]string)
	for _, rc := range changes {
		if rc.Action == plans.NoOp {
			continue
		}
		addr := rc.Addr.String()
		grouped[rc.Action] = append(grouped[rc.Action], addr)
	}

	if len(grouped) == 0 {
		return "No changes.\n"
	}

	// Define action display order
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.Read,
	}

	var buf strings.Builder
	var summaryParts []string

	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		addrs, ok := grouped[action]
		if !ok {
			continue
		}
		sort.Strings(addrs)
		label := actionLabel(action)
		for _, addr := range addrs {
			fmt.Fprintf(&buf, "[%s] %s\n", label, addr)
		}
		summaryParts = append(summaryParts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to %s", len(addrs), label))
	}

	buf.WriteString("\n")
	fmt.Fprintf(&buf, "Plan: %s.\n", strings.Join(summaryParts, ", "))

	return b
... (truncated)
2. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact_test.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
)

func mustParseResourceInstanceAddr(s string) addrs.AbsResourceInstance {
	addr, diags := addrs.ParseAbsResourceInstanceStr(s)
	if diags.HasErrors() {
		panic(diags.Err().Error())
	}
	return addr
}

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format_NilPlan(t *testing.T) {
	f := &CompactDiffFormatter{}
	result := f.Format(nil, nil)
	if result != "No changes.\n" {
		t.Errorf("expected 'No changes.\\n', got %q", result)
	}
}

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format_EmptyChanges(t *testing.T) {
	f := &CompactDiffFormatter{}
	plan := &plans.Plan{
		Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{},
	}
	result := f.Format(plan, nil)
	if result != "No changes.\n" {
		t.Errorf("expected 'No changes.\\n', got %q", result)
	}
}

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format_NoopExcluded(t *testing.T) {
	f := &CompactDiffFormatter{}
	addr := mustParseResourceInstanceAddr("aws_instance.noop")
	plan := &plans.Plan{
		Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
			Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
				{
					Addr:      addr,
					ChangeSrc: plans.ChangeSrc{Action: plans.NoOp},
				},
			},
		},
	}
	result := f.Format(plan, nil)
	if result != "No changes.\n" {
		t.Errorf("expected 'No changes.\\n' for noop plan, got %q", result)
	}
}

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format_CreateAction(t *testing.T) {
	f := &CompactDiffFormatter{}
	addr := mustParseResourceInstanceAddr("aws_instance.foo")
	plan := &plans.Plan{
		Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
			Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
				{
					Addr:      addr,
					ChangeSrc: plans.ChangeSrc{Action: plans.Create},
				},
			},
		},
	}
	result := f.Format(plan, nil
